	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading mw-first-heading">NIFTY 50</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="vector-body">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		<div id="contentSub2"></div>
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" lang="en" dir="ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Indian stock market index</div>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1033289096">.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}</style><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">For the informal 1960s US stock market designation, see <a href="/wiki/Nifty_Fifty" title="Nifty Fifty">Nifty Fifty</a>.</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1066479718">.mw-parser-output .infobox-subbox{padding:0;border:none;margin:-3px;width:auto;min-width:100%;font-size:100%;clear:none;float:none;background-color:transparent}.mw-parser-output .infobox-subheader,body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .infobox-above,body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .infobox-title,body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .infobox-image,body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .infobox-full-data,body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .infobox-below{text-align:center}</style><table class="infobox vcard"><caption class="infobox-title fn n org">NIFTY NIFTY 50 index between 1990 and 2021</div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Foundation</th><td class="infobox-data">21 April 1997</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" href="/wiki/Capitalization-weighted_index" title="Capitalization-weighted index">Capitalisation-weighted</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Website</th><td class="infobox-data"><span class="url"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.nseindia.com/">www<wbr />.nseindia<wbr />.com</a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>NIFTY 50</b> is a benchmark <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> <a href="/wiki/Stock_market_index" title="Stock market index">stock market index</a> that represents the weighted average of 50 of the largest Indian companies listed on the <a href="/wiki/National_Stock_Exchange_of_India" title="National Stock Exchange of India">National Stock Exchange</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> It is one of the two main stock indices used in India, the other being the <a href="/wiki/BSE_SENSEX" title="BSE SENSEX">BSE SENSEX</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-nse_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nse-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nifty 50 is owned and managed by <a href="/wiki/NSE_Indices" title="NSE Indices">NSE Indices</a> (previously known as India Index Services &amp; Products Limited), which is a wholly owned subsidiary of the NSE Strategic Investment Corporation Limited.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/NSE_Indices" title="NSE Indices">NSE Indices</a> had a marketing and licensing agreement with <a href="/wiki/Standard_%26_Poor%27s" class="mw-redirect" title="Standard &amp; Poor&#39;s">Standard &amp; Poor's</a> for co-branding equity indices until 2013. The Nifty 50 index was launched on 22 April 1996,<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> and is one of the many stock indices of Nifty.
</p><p>The NIFTY 50 index has shaped up to be the largest single financial product in India, with an ecosystem consisting of <a href="/wiki/Exchange-traded_fund" title="Exchange-traded fund">exchange-traded funds</a> (onshore and offshore), exchange-traded options at <a href="/wiki/National_Stock_Exchange_of_India" title="National Stock Exchange of India">NSE</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> and futures and options abroad at the <a href="/wiki/Singapore_Exchange" title="Singapore Exchange">SGX</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> NIFTY 50 is the world's most actively traded contract. WFE, IOM and FIA surveys endorse NSE's leadership position.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The NIFTY 50 index covers 13 sectors (as on 30 April 2021) of the <a href="/wiki/Indian_economy" class="mw-redirect" title="Indian economy">Indian economy</a> and offers investment managers exposure to the Indian market in one portfolio. Between 2008 &amp; 2012, the NIFTY 50 index's share of <a href="/wiki/National_Stock_Exchange_of_India" title="National Stock Exchange of India">NSE's</a> market capitalisation fell from 65% to 29%<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> due to the rise of sectoral indices like NIFTY Bank, NIFTY IT, NIFTY Pharma, NIFTY SERV SECTOR, NIFTY Next 50, etc. The NIFTY 50 Index gives a weightage of 39.47% to <a href="/wiki/Financial_services" title="Financial services">financial services</a>, 15.31% to <a href="/wiki/Energy_industry" title="Energy industry">Energy</a>, 13.01% to <a href="/wiki/Information_technology" title="Information technology">IT</a>, 12.38% to <a href="/wiki/Fast-moving_consumer_goods" title="Fast-moving consumer goods">consumer goods</a>, 6.11% to <a href="/wiki/Automobiles" class="mw-redirect" title="Automobiles">Automobiles</a> and 0% to the <a href="/wiki/Agriculture" title="Agriculture">agricultural sector</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The NIFTY 50 index is a <a href="/wiki/Capitalization-weighted_index" title="Capitalization-weighted index">free float market capitalisation weighted index</a>. The index was initially calculated on a full market capitalisation methodology. On 26 June 2009, the computation was changed to a free-float methodology.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> The base period for the NIFTY 50 index is 3 November 1995, which marked the completion of one year of operations of the <i>National Stock Exchange Equity Market Segment</i>. The base value of the index has been set at 1000 and a base capital of ₹ 2.06&#160;trillion.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<td>24.12
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Derivatives">Derivatives</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=NIFTY_50&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Derivatives">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Trading in <a href="/wiki/Call_option" title="Call option">call</a> and <a href="/wiki/Put_option" title="Put option">put</a> options on the Nifty 50 are offered by the NSE.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> The exchange offers weekly as well as monthly expiry.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="NIFTY_Next_50">NIFTY Next 50</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=NIFTY_50&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: NIFTY Next 50">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096"/><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/NIFTY_Next_50" title="NIFTY Next 50">NIFTY Next 50</a></div>
<p>NIFTY Next 50, also called NIFTY Junior, is an index of 50 companies whose free float market capitalisation comes after that of the companies in NIFTY 50. NIFTY Next 50 constituents are thus potential candidates for future inclusion in NIFTY 50.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
